    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [ProductPresentations] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]

    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [ProductPresentations] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]

    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]

    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0

LEFT JOIN [ProductPresentations] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]

    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]

    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]

    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [ProductPresentations] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [ProductPresentations] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [ProductPresentations] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[AllowPromotions], [p].[AutoMarkSoldOut], [p].[BranchId], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CatalogBadge], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreatedOnUtc], [p].[CurrentCost], [p].[DefaultUnitOfMeasureId], [p].[Description], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[FavoriteOrder], [p].[HighlightInCatalog], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[InternalCode], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsCatalogVisible], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsFavorite], [p].[IsSoldOut], [p].[LastModifiedBy], [p].[LastModifiedOnUtc], [p].[MinimumStock], [p].[Name], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductType], [p].[RequiresBatchControl], [p].[RequiresSerialNumber], [p].[ShortDescription], [p].[SoldOutAt], [p].[SoldOutBy], [p].[TaxId], [p].[TrackInventory]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[InternalCode] = @__data_Code_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [ProductPresentations] AS [p0] ON [t].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id]
